   tāṃ suratasukhasantuṣṭāmapaśyat /	tAm surata-suKa-santuzwAm-apaSyat /
   "paropabhuktadeheyam' iti tāṃ dṛṣṭāṃ matvā sāvaśyaṃ vadhyeti niścitya	"para-upaBukta-dehA-iyam-a iti tAm dRzwAm matvA sa-avaSyam vaDyA-iti niScitya
   caṇḍikālayaṃ yayau /	caNxikA-Alayam yayO /
   yāvattadagrato mārayati tāvadanyayā phūtkṛtam-"svāmini! mama tvayā varo	yAvat-tat-agratas mArayati tAvat-anyayA PUtkRtam--"svAmini! mama tvayA varaH-
   datto yattava gandharvacakravartī putro bhaviṣyati /	dattaH yat-tava ganDarva-cakravartI putraH Bavizyati /
   tatkathaṃ putramukhama dṛṣṭvā vipatsye' /	tat-kaTam putra-muKama dRzwvA vipatsye-a /
   evaṃ vilapantyāstasyāḥ puratastāṃ prati devī prāha-he gandharvavīra!	evam vilapantyAH-tasyAH puratas-tAm prati devI prAha-he ganDarva-vIra!
   nāsyāḥ ko 'pi doṣaḥ /	na-asyAH kaH api dozaH /
   kintu vidyādhareṇeyaṃ tvadīyarūpamayena māyayā bhuktā /	kintu vidyADareNa-iyam tvadIya-rUpa-mayena mAyayA BuktA /
   tato 'jānantyā asyā na doṣaḥ /	tatas ajAnantyAH asyAH na dozaH /
   anyacca muniśāpo vidyate /	anyat-ca muni-SApaH vidyate /
   tata idaṃ sañjātam-"śāpavṛttāntaśca niveditaḥ, tato munivacanādiyaṃ	tatas idam saQjAtam-"-SApa-vRttAntaH-ca niveditaH, tatas muni-vacanAt-iyam
   nirdeṣā tvayā grāhyā'-iti gaurīvacanaṃ śrutvā sa niḥśaṅkaṃ tayā saha	nirdezA tvayA grAhyA-a-iti gOrI-vacanam SrutvA sa niHSaFkam tayA saha
   svasthānaṃ gatastathaiva sukhato 'bhūt" /	sva-sTAnam gataH-taTA-eva suKataH aBUt" /
   tato vaṇikputra /	tatas vaNij-putra /
   yadi madvacaḥ pramāṇaṃ tadaināmaduṣṭāṃ prati prasādaṃ kartumarhasi' /	yadi mad-vacaH pramANam tadEnAma-duzwAm prati prasAdam kartum-arhasi-a /
   iti kīravacanānmadanenānugṛhītā /	iti kIra-vacanAt-madanena-anugRhItA /
   tato haridatto 'pi putrāgamanatuṣṭo mahotsavaṃ cakāra /	tatas haridattaH api putra-Agamana-tuzwaH mahA-utsavam cakAra /
   tasminmahotsave divyamālā patitā /	tasmin-mahA-utsave divya-mAlA patitA /
   taddarśane śukasārikātrivikramāṇāṃ śāpamokṣātsvargagamanaṃ babhūva /	tad-darSane Suka-sArikA-trivikramANAm SApa-mokzAt-svarga-gamanam baBUva /
   madano 'pi priyayā prabhāvatyā saha sukhāni bhuṅkte /	madanaH api priyayA praBAvatyA saha suKAni BuFkte /
   iti śukasaptatau saptatitamī kathā /	iti Suka-saptatO saptatitamI kaTA /
   iti śukasaptatiḥ samāptā //	iti SukasaptatiH samAptAH //
